***чихать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чихать.html>чиха́ть</a> (11965)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čixati</i>, of onomatopoeic origin. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">чи́хамь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">číhamʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (Gerov), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">číhati</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tonal orthography</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> (1sg. <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">čȋham</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tonal orthography</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Upper_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Upper Sorbian language">Upper Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hsb">čichać</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">tśichaś</i>. Also found as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">чхать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čьxati</i>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">чха́ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čxáty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">чхаць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čxacʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">czchać</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чихать.html>чиха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čixátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чихнуть.html>чихну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sneeze</li>
<li>to scorn, to disdain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чихать.html>чиха́ть</a></b> <i>(<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a>)</i></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne <b>čixátʹ</b> <i>(na)</i></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I don't give a damn <i>(for)</i>, I don't care a button <i>(about)</i></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">апчхи́</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">apčxí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чих.html>чих</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">čix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">чиха́ние</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">čixánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">чихательный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">čixatelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***член.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:член.html>член</a> (677)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">*члѣнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*člěnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čelnъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kel-</i> / <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷel-</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-nъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:член.html>член</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">člen</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:член.html>чле́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:член.html>чле́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:член.html>чле́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>limb</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> article
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">арти́кль</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">artíklʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>part</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> term</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> member of an organization</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> penis
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:головка.html>голо́вка</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тело.html>те́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:половой.html>полово́го</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:член.html>чле́на</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:содержать.html>соде́ржит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:множество.html>мно́жество</a> лаку́н, <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:половой.html>полово́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:возбуждение.html>возбужде́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заполняющийся.html>заполня́ющихся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровь.html>кро́вью</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:кроме.html>кро́ме</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ней</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:иметься.html>име́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:количество.html>коли́чество</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нервный.html>не́рвных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ний</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лает</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наиболее.html>наибо́лее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувствительный.html>чувстви́тельной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>ча́стью</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:член.html>чле́на</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Golóvka, kak i télo polovóvo <b>čléna</b>, sodéržit mnóžestvo lakún, pri polovóm vozbuždénii zapolnjájuščixsja króvʹju. Króme tovó, na nej iméjetsja bolʹšóje kolíčestvo nérvnyx okončánij, što délajet jejó naibóleje čuvstvítelʹnoj částʹju <b>čléna</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The glans, like the body of the penis, contains a number of cavities that fill with blood during sexual arousal. In addition, it has a large number of nerve endings, which makes it the most sensitive part of the penis.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

***чокнуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чокнуться.html>чо́кнуться</a> (12154)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чокаться.html>чо́каться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čókatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чокнуться.html>чо́кнуться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čóknutʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чокаться.html>чо́каться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go nuts, to get cranky <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to become mad</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to clink glasses (with), to touch glasses (when drinking alcohol)</li></ol>

***чопорный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чопорный.html>чо́порный</a> (26142)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From an unattested Old East Slavic word + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare Russian Church Slavic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">чепрь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čeprĭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">delight, pleasure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Also cognate with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">чепори́ться</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čeporítʹsja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be important</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">чепури́ться</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čepurítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">чепу́риться</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čepúritʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), and similarly with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">чепури́ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čepurýty</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dress up, to decorate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">чепу́рити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čepúryty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">чепури́тися</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čepurýtysja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be important</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">чепу́ритися</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čepúrytysja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">чепуры́цца</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čjepurýcca</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be important</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">čepériti se</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bristle one's feathers, to be important</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tonal orthography</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language">Greek</a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">τσοπορός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tsoporós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cutesy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (a borrowing from Slavic).
</p>

***чрево.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чрево.html>чре́во</a> (14893)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">чрѣво</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">črěvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*červo</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">черёво</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čerjóvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чрево.html>чре́во</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">črévo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чрево.html>чре́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чрево.html>чре́ва</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чрево.html>чре́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> belly, womb</li>
<li>inside, interior</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чрезмерный.html>чрезме́рный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">črezmérnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чресла.html>чре́сла</a> (32416)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">чрѣсла</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">črěsla</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čerslo</i>. Displaced the native East Slavic form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">че́ресла</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čéresla</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> reins, small of the back</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">чт-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čt-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чтение.html>чте́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čténije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чтение.html>чте́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чтение.html>чте́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чтение.html>чте́ний</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чтиво.html>чти́во</a> (31450)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">чт-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čt-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-иво</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(material)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. For the root, compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:честь.html>чту́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čtu</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I read</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чтивший.html>чти́вший</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čtívšij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">having read</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, etc. For the ending, compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:месиво.html>ме́сиво</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mésivo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jumble, mush</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">моло́зиво</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">molózivo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">colostrum (type of breast milk)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чтиво.html>чти́во</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čtívo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чтиво.html>чти́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чтиво.html>чти́ва</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:честь.html>чти́в</a></b>)
</p>

***чтить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чтить.html>чти́ть</a> (14021)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čьstiti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)kʷit-tis</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">чтити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čtyty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">czcić</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чтить.html>чти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čtitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почтить.html>почти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to honor, to revere</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***что.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> (112)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čьto</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷid</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">što</span>) <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">invariable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>that
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́маю</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́ма</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja dúmaju, <b>što</b> on dóma.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I think <b>that</b> he's home.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">što</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">interrogative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> what
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>Что</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Što</b> éto?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>What</b> is this?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ет</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значить.html>зна́чит</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On ne znájet, <b>što</b> éto znáčit.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He doesn’t know <b>what</b> this means.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nonstandard<span class="ib-comma">,</span> relative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> that, which
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́га</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>столе́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kníga, <b>što</b> na stolé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the book <b>that</b> is on the table</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>In informal speech, the genitive form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чего́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čevó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> often replaces the accusative and sometimes the nominative.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">чё</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">čo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">чо</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">čo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">interrogative pronoun only, non-standard, highly colloquial but common, not used in writing</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a> <b>чё</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пошли́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nu <b>čó</b>, pošlí, štó li?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Well, let's go!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b>Чё</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хо́чет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Čó</b> on xóčet ot menjá?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What (the hell) does he want from me?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">шо</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">šo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">same as above, used in the South of European Russia or by Russian speakers in Ukraine</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kotóryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">standard relative pronoun</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>

***чтобы.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>чтобы</a> (70)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">što</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">by</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štóby</span>) <i>(+ past tense or the infinitive)</i>
</p>
<ol><li>that...should (<span class="use-with-mention">indicates the subjunctive</span>)</li>
<li>so that, in order that; in order to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невозможно.html>невозмо́жно</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лала</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nevozmóžno, <b>štóby</b> oná éto sdélala</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It’s impossible that she should have done this; She could not possibly have done this.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вовремя.html>во́время</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>štóby</b> bytʹ vóvremja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in order to be on time.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>lest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:забыть.html>забы́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>štóby</b> ja ne zabýl</i> ― <span class="e-translation">lest I forget; so that I won’t forget.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>perceptional, sensory
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чувственный.html>чу́вственное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:восприятие.html>восприя́тие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čúvstvennoje</b> vosprijátije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sensory perception</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>sensual
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чувственный.html>чу́вственные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>гу́бы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čúvstvennyje</b> gúby</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sensual lips</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
